# Top 50 Throwers / Throwing Athletes Exercise Cards

## Source and caveat

- exercise_card_details_for_llm.md: Card v2 authoring workflow, canonical phase keys, movement identity, taxonomy key+weight tags, movement requirements, why layer, coaching execution, dosage, scaling cohorts, pairing logic, safety, regimen, and phase profile.
- Purpose.txt status: requested and searched for, but no accessible File Library result surfaced a file literally titled Purpose.txt during this run. This caveat is preserved in every generated file rather than pretending the file was read.
- Sport-science basis: overhead throwing is treated as a full kinetic-chain task, with selections covering lower body force, hip-pelvis-trunk transfer, scapular control, shoulder/elbow/forearm capacity, rotational power, and fatigue-safe practice design.

## Evidence basis

- Kinetic chain: throwing performance and shoulder/elbow stress are influenced by linked contribution from lower extremity, hip/pelvis, trunk, scapulothoracic, shoulder/elbow, and distal segments.
- Training adaptation: resistance-based training and medicine-ball/rotational power work are used because throwing velocity depends on force generation, force transfer, and high-intent low-fatigue expression.
- Injury-risk management: the library includes scapular, rotator-cuff, elbow/forearm, trunk, and lower-body control work because throwing athletes often need both output and tissue capacity.
- Programming rule: high-speed throws, sprints, bounds, and medicine-ball outputs stay early, low volume, and fully rested; strength and tissue capacity are separated from skill throws when fatigue would corrupt mechanics.

## Top 50 by category

### 01-10 - Throwing Mobility, Rib-Scap Access, and Activation
Low-fatigue drills that open thoracic rotation, hip access, shoulder flexion, scapular motion, cuff readiness, and rib-pelvis stacking before throwing or lifting.

01. **Half-Kneeling T-Spine Rotation Reach** - Half-Kneeling T-Spine Rotation Reach is a throwing-athlete exercise for opens thoracic rotation while the pelvis is constrained so throwers can rotate above a stable base instead of stealing motion from the low back.
02. **Open Book T-Spine Rotation** - Open Book T-Spine Rotation is a throwing-athlete exercise for restores gentle rib and thoracic rotation for athletes who feel locked up before throwing, batting, serving, or overhead work.
03. **Adductor Rock-Back with T-Spine Reach** - Adductor Rock-Back with T-Spine Reach is a throwing-athlete exercise for combines adductor length, hip hinge access, and rotation so the athlete can separate hips and trunk cleanly.
04. **Half-Kneeling Hip Flexor Reach** - Half-Kneeling Hip Flexor Reach is a throwing-athlete exercise for improves front-hip extension and rib position for stride length, pelvis control, and cleaner trunk rotation.
05. **Wall Slide with Lift-Off** - Wall Slide with Lift-Off is a throwing-athlete exercise for builds active shoulder flexion and upward rotation without letting the ribs flare or neck take over.
06. **Serratus Foam-Roller Wall Slide** - Serratus Foam-Roller Wall Slide is a throwing-athlete exercise for primes serratus anterior, scapular upward rotation, and rib control for safer overhead reach and follow-through.
07. **Quadruped Scapular Clock** - Quadruped Scapular Clock is a throwing-athlete exercise for teaches the athlete to move and feel the scapula without bending the elbow or dumping into the neck.
08. **Band Pull-Apart to W** - Band Pull-Apart to W is a throwing-athlete exercise for wakes up posterior shoulder and mid-back tissues before throwing or pressing without heavy fatigue.
09. **Band 90/90 External Rotation Activation** - Band 90/90 External Rotation Activation is a throwing-athlete exercise for primes cuff control in the abducted throwing position while keeping load low and motion crisp.
10. **Dead Bug Pullover with Exhale** - Dead Bug Pullover with Exhale is a throwing-athlete exercise for connects trunk brace, exhale, lat length, and shoulder flexion so the athlete can reach without lumbar extension.

### 11-20 - Rotational and Medicine-Ball Throwing Power
High-intent, low-rep throws that train hip-to-trunk sequencing, bracing, arm-speed expression, catch readiness, and rotational force transfer without conditioning creep.

11. **Standing Medicine Ball Scoop Toss** - Standing Medicine Ball Scoop Toss is a throwing-athlete exercise for foundational rotational throw that links back hip load, trunk turn, and fast release with a simple setup.
12. **Step-Behind Rotational Medicine Ball Throw** - Step-Behind Rotational Medicine Ball Throw is a throwing-athlete exercise for adds approach momentum so throwers practice loading the rear hip and transferring force into release.
13. **Shuffle-to-Rotational Medicine Ball Throw** - Shuffle-to-Rotational Medicine Ball Throw is a throwing-athlete exercise for teaches rhythm from lateral footwork into hip-shoulder separation and fast trunk delivery.
14. **Split-Stance Medicine Ball Shot-Put Pass** - Split-Stance Medicine Ball Shot-Put Pass is a throwing-athlete exercise for builds single-arm power, front-side brace, and trunk rotation without requiring a full throw.
15. **Kneeling Medicine Ball Chest Pass** - Kneeling Medicine Ball Chest Pass is a throwing-athlete exercise for removes leg drive so the coach can see trunk stiffness, shoulder speed, and release quality.
16. **Tall-Kneeling Overhead Medicine Ball Slam** - Tall-Kneeling Overhead Medicine Ball Slam is a throwing-athlete exercise for trains rapid trunk flexion and overhead force expression while limiting lower-body compensation.
17. **Medicine Ball Rebound Slam to Catch** - Medicine Ball Rebound Slam to Catch is a throwing-athlete exercise for blends force absorption and re-output through hands, trunk, and shoulders with a clear catch quality gate.
18. **Countermovement Medicine Ball Scoop Toss** - Countermovement Medicine Ball Scoop Toss is a throwing-athlete exercise for uses a controlled countermovement to train elastic pre-load before a fast rotational release.
19. **Lateral Bound to Rotational Throw** - Lateral Bound to Rotational Throw is a throwing-athlete exercise for connects lateral projection, landing stiffness, hip capture, and rotational throw transfer.
20. **Partner Reactive Medicine Ball Toss and Relocate** - Partner Reactive Medicine Ball Toss and Relocate is a throwing-athlete exercise for adds live timing, relocation footwork, visual tracking, and catch posture without turning throws into conditioning.

### 21-30 - Lower-Body Force, Braking, Sprint, and Transfer
Strength, acceleration, lateral force, and deceleration options that build the legs and hips that initiate and stabilize a throw.

21. **Trap Bar Deadlift** - Trap Bar Deadlift is a throwing-athlete exercise for builds general hip and leg force with a shoulder-friendly grip position for athletes who need strength without excessive spinal or shoulder stress.
22. **Front Squat** - Front Squat is a throwing-athlete exercise for trains leg drive and trunk stiffness in an upright posture that carries to blocking, bracing, and staying tall through the throw.
23. **Rear-Foot-Elevated Split Squat** - Rear-Foot-Elevated Split Squat is a throwing-athlete exercise for targets stride-leg strength, hip stability, and asymmetry management with a thrower-relevant split stance.
24. **Lateral Lunge** - Lateral Lunge is a throwing-athlete exercise for builds lateral hip strength and adductor tolerance for rotational athletes who load and shift side-to-side.
25. **Single-Leg Romanian Deadlift** - Single-Leg Romanian Deadlift is a throwing-athlete exercise for trains hamstring-glute strength, hip hinge control, and balance for landing, stride, and fielding transfer.
26. **Hip Thrust** - Hip Thrust is a throwing-athlete exercise for develops hip extension force without loading the shoulder in an overhead position.
27. **Sled Push Acceleration** - Sled Push Acceleration is a throwing-athlete exercise for builds early acceleration angles and lower-body force projection while keeping running mechanics simple.
28. **Lateral Sled Drag** - Lateral Sled Drag is a throwing-athlete exercise for loads lateral hip drive and trunk posture for throwers who need force transfer across the frontal plane.
29. **10-Yard Sprint Start** - 10-Yard Sprint Start is a throwing-athlete exercise for short acceleration exposure builds nervous-system output and leg drive without excessive running volume.
30. **Lateral Bound to Stick** - Lateral Bound to Stick is a throwing-athlete exercise for trains lateral projection, hip capture, knee alignment, and quiet landings before higher-intent lateral power.

### 31-40 - Trunk, Pelvis, Anti-Rotation, and Force Transmission
Core and trunk-pelvis drills that teach athletes to transfer force from ground to hand while resisting leaks, over-rotation, extension, and side-bending collapse.

31. **Pallof Press Iso Hold** - Pallof Press Iso Hold is a throwing-athlete exercise for teaches the athlete to resist unwanted trunk rotation while breathing and keeping pelvis-rib alignment.
32. **Half-Kneeling Cable Lift** - Half-Kneeling Cable Lift is a throwing-athlete exercise for trains diagonal force transfer from hip through trunk to hands while the pelvis stays organized.
33. **Half-Kneeling Cable Chop** - Half-Kneeling Cable Chop is a throwing-athlete exercise for builds controlled trunk rotation and anti-extension in a split stance relevant to throwing posture.
34. **Landmine Anti-Rotation Press** - Landmine Anti-Rotation Press is a throwing-athlete exercise for develops trunk stiffness and scapular upward reach through an angled press that is usually more shoulder-friendly than full overhead pressing.
35. **Cable Anti-Rotation Step-Out** - Cable Anti-Rotation Step-Out is a throwing-athlete exercise for adds controlled footwork to anti-rotation so athletes learn to keep trunk position while stepping into and out of tension.
36. **Suitcase Carry** - Suitcase Carry is a throwing-athlete exercise for builds lateral trunk stiffness, grip, and gait posture without repetitive throwing stress.
37. **Farmer Carry** - Farmer Carry is a throwing-athlete exercise for builds grip, shoulder depression control, trunk stiffness, and total-body work capacity in a simple pattern.
38. **Side Plank Row** - Side Plank Row is a throwing-athlete exercise for combines lateral trunk control with scapular rowing, useful for throwers who leak through ribs or pelvis while pulling.
39. **Bird Dog Row** - Bird Dog Row is a throwing-athlete exercise for links contralateral trunk stability, hip control, and scapular pull without speed or impact.
40. **Stir-the-Pot Plank** - Stir-the-Pot Plank is a throwing-athlete exercise for challenges trunk anti-extension and shoulder support under small moving perturbations.

### 41-50 - Shoulder, Scapular, Elbow, and Forearm Capacity
Targeted tissue-capacity work for the cuff, scapular stabilizers, elbow, wrist, and forearm that supports repeated throwing without replacing skill-specific throwing exposure.

41. **Prone Y-T-W Raise** - Prone Y-T-W Raise is a throwing-athlete exercise for builds low-load scapular retraction, upward rotation, and posterior shoulder control for throwers.
42. **Face Pull to External Rotation** - Face Pull to External Rotation is a throwing-athlete exercise for combines upper-back pull with external rotation control without heavy pressing stress.
43. **Cable or Band 90/90 External Rotation** - Cable or Band 90/90 External Rotation is a throwing-athlete exercise for builds cuff strength and control in the abducted position used near the arm-cocking phase.
44. **Eccentric Band External Rotation** - Eccentric Band External Rotation is a throwing-athlete exercise for emphasizes slow external-rotation lowering to support deceleration tolerance after ball release.
45. **Band Shoulder Internal Rotation Decel Control** - Band Shoulder Internal Rotation Decel Control is a throwing-athlete exercise for trains controlled shoulder rotation through a safe range so the athlete owns the motion instead of snapping through it.
46. **Bottoms-Up Kettlebell Carry** - Bottoms-Up Kettlebell Carry is a throwing-athlete exercise for builds reflexive cuff, scapular, wrist, and grip stability with low reps and high attention.
47. **Landmine Press** - Landmine Press is a throwing-athlete exercise for strengthens pressing and upward reach on an angled path that many throwers tolerate better than vertical pressing.
48. **Chin-Up or Assisted Chin-Up** - Chin-Up or Assisted Chin-Up is a throwing-athlete exercise for builds lat, upper-back, grip, and shoulder control when the athlete can keep ribs and neck organized.
49. **Wrist Pronation-Supination Hammer Control** - Wrist Pronation-Supination Hammer Control is a throwing-athlete exercise for targets forearm pronation-supination control for elbow and wrist tolerance in repeated throwing.
50. **Forearm Flexor/Extensor Eccentric** - Forearm Flexor/Extensor Eccentric is a throwing-athlete exercise for builds local forearm tolerance through slow eccentrics, useful as support work for high-volume throwers.

# Throwers / Throwing Athletes Exercise Cards 01-10

## Category focus: Throwing Mobility, Rib-Scap Access, and Activation
Low-fatigue drills that open thoracic rotation, hip access, shoulder flexion, scapular motion, cuff readiness, and rib-pelvis stacking before throwing or lifting.

## Exercises in this batch

01. **Half-Kneeling T-Spine Rotation Reach** - `prepare_and_access` / `mobilize` / `t_spine_rotation_access` - Opens thoracic rotation while the pelvis is constrained so throwers can rotate above a stable base instead of stealing motion from the low back.
02. **Open Book T-Spine Rotation** - `prepare_and_access` / `mobilize` / `open_book_rotation` - Restores gentle rib and thoracic rotation for athletes who feel locked up before throwing, batting, serving, or overhead work.
03. **Adductor Rock-Back with T-Spine Reach** - `prepare_and_access` / `mobilize` / `adductor_rockback_t_spine_reach` - Combines adductor length, hip hinge access, and rotation so the athlete can separate hips and trunk cleanly.
04. **Half-Kneeling Hip Flexor Reach** - `prepare_and_access` / `mobilize` / `hip_flexor_reach_throwing_prep` - Improves front-hip extension and rib position for stride length, pelvis control, and cleaner trunk rotation.
05. **Wall Slide with Lift-Off** - `prepare_and_access` / `mobilize` / `wall_slide_lift_off_overhead_access` - Builds active shoulder flexion and upward rotation without letting the ribs flare or neck take over.
06. **Serratus Foam-Roller Wall Slide** - `prepare_and_access` / `activate` / `serratus_wall_slide` - Primes serratus anterior, scapular upward rotation, and rib control for safer overhead reach and follow-through.
07. **Quadruped Scapular Clock** - `prepare_and_access` / `activate` / `quadruped_scapular_clock` - Teaches the athlete to move and feel the scapula without bending the elbow or dumping into the neck.
08. **Band Pull-Apart to W** - `prepare_and_access` / `activate` / `band_pull_apart_to_w` - Wakes up posterior shoulder and mid-back tissues before throwing or pressing without heavy fatigue.
09. **Band 90/90 External Rotation Activation** - `prepare_and_access` / `activate` / `band_90_90_external_rotation_activation` - Primes cuff control in the abducted throwing position while keeping load low and motion crisp.
10. **Dead Bug Pullover with Exhale** - `prepare_and_access` / `activate` / `dead_bug_pullover_exhale` - Connects trunk brace, exhale, lat length, and shoulder flexion so the athlete can reach without lumbar extension.

# Throwers / Throwing Athletes Exercise Cards 11-20

## Source and authoring basis

- exercise_card_details_for_llm.md: Card v2 authoring workflow, canonical phase keys, movement identity, taxonomy key+weight tags, movement requirements, why layer, coaching execution, dosage, scaling cohorts, pairing logic, safety, regimen, and phase profile.
- Purpose.txt status: requested and searched for, but no accessible File Library result surfaced a file literally titled Purpose.txt during this run. This caveat is preserved in every generated file rather than pretending the file was read.
- Sport-science basis: overhead throwing is treated as a full kinetic-chain task, with selections covering lower body force, hip-pelvis-trunk transfer, scapular control, shoulder/elbow/forearm capacity, rotational power, and fatigue-safe practice design.

## Category focus: Rotational and Medicine-Ball Throwing Power
High-intent, low-rep throws that train hip-to-trunk sequencing, bracing, arm-speed expression, catch readiness, and rotational force transfer without conditioning creep.

## Exercises in this batch

11. **Standing Medicine Ball Scoop Toss** - `output` / `jump_throw_explosive_power` / `standing_med_ball_scoop_toss` - Foundational rotational throw that links back hip load, trunk turn, and fast release with a simple setup.
12. **Step-Behind Rotational Medicine Ball Throw** - `output` / `jump_throw_explosive_power` / `step_behind_rotational_med_ball_throw` - Adds approach momentum so throwers practice loading the rear hip and transferring force into release.
13. **Shuffle-to-Rotational Medicine Ball Throw** - `output` / `jump_throw_explosive_power` / `shuffle_rotational_med_ball_throw` - Teaches rhythm from lateral footwork into hip-shoulder separation and fast trunk delivery.
14. **Split-Stance Medicine Ball Shot-Put Pass** - `output` / `jump_throw_explosive_power` / `split_stance_med_ball_shot_put_pass` - Builds single-arm power, front-side brace, and trunk rotation without requiring a full throw.
15. **Kneeling Medicine Ball Chest Pass** - `output` / `jump_throw_explosive_power` / `kneeling_med_ball_chest_pass` - Removes leg drive so the coach can see trunk stiffness, shoulder speed, and release quality.
16. **Tall-Kneeling Overhead Medicine Ball Slam** - `output` / `jump_throw_explosive_power` / `tall_kneeling_overhead_med_ball_slam` - Trains rapid trunk flexion and overhead force expression while limiting lower-body compensation.
17. **Medicine Ball Rebound Slam to Catch** - `output` / `jump_throw_explosive_power` / `med_ball_rebound_slam_catch` - Blends force absorption and re-output through hands, trunk, and shoulders with a clear catch quality gate.
18. **Countermovement Medicine Ball Scoop Toss** - `output` / `jump_throw_explosive_power` / `countermovement_med_ball_scoop_toss` - Uses a controlled countermovement to train elastic pre-load before a fast rotational release.
19. **Lateral Bound to Rotational Throw** - `output` / `jump_throw_explosive_power` / `lateral_bound_to_rotational_throw` - Connects lateral projection, landing stiffness, hip capture, and rotational throw transfer.
20. **Partner Reactive Medicine Ball Toss and Relocate** - `movement_intelligence` / `perception_action_skill` / `partner_reactive_med_ball_toss_relocate_throwers` - Adds live timing, relocation footwork, visual tracking, and catch posture without turning throws into conditioning.

          "Select a clear space and set up medicine ball, partner, cones.",
          "Use a load, range, or speed that lets the athlete move without pain or compensation.",
          "Confirm the athlete can breathe, brace, and keep neck, ribs, pelvis, and throwing-side shoulder organized before the first rep."
        ],
        "execution_steps": [
          "Explain the cue, target, partner role, or decision rule before the first rep.",
          "Move at a speed that allows accurate information pickup and clean body organization.",
          "Complete the throw, catch, relocation, or reset with balance and safe spacing.",
          "Progress only one variable at a time: speed, distance, load, cue complexity, or partner pressure."
        ],
        "coach_cues": [
          "See it first, then move.",
          "Throw, relocate, catch, reset.",
          "Quality beats speed."
        ],
        "common_faults": [
          "Guessing before the cue.",
          "Colliding, crowding the partner, or losing spacing.",
          "Repeating after decision quality or catching posture degrades."
        ],
        "breathing_cues": [
          "Exhale to set the ribs before effort.",
          "Breathe between reps; do not hold your breath through setup and reset."
        ],
        "quality_gate": "Rep passes only if the athlete reads the cue, chooses the correct answer, moves safely, and resets before fatigue noise.",

# Throwers / Throwing Athletes Exercise Cards 21-30

## Source and authoring basis

- exercise_card_details_for_llm.md: Card v2 authoring workflow, canonical phase keys, movement identity, taxonomy key+weight tags, movement requirements, why layer, coaching execution, dosage, scaling cohorts, pairing logic, safety, regimen, and phase profile.
- Purpose.txt status: requested and searched for, but no accessible File Library result surfaced a file literally titled Purpose.txt during this run. This caveat is preserved in every generated file rather than pretending the file was read.
- Sport-science basis: overhead throwing is treated as a full kinetic-chain task, with selections covering lower body force, hip-pelvis-trunk transfer, scapular control, shoulder/elbow/forearm capacity, rotational power, and fatigue-safe practice design.

## Category focus: Lower-Body Force, Braking, Sprint, and Transfer
Strength, acceleration, lateral force, and deceleration options that build the legs and hips that initiate and stabilize a throw.

## Exercises in this batch

21. **Trap Bar Deadlift** - `capacity` / `lower_body_strength` / `trap_bar_deadlift_throwers` - Builds general hip and leg force with a shoulder-friendly grip position for athletes who need strength without excessive spinal or shoulder stress.
22. **Front Squat** - `capacity` / `lower_body_strength` / `front_squat_throwers` - Trains leg drive and trunk stiffness in an upright posture that carries to blocking, bracing, and staying tall through the throw.
23. **Rear-Foot-Elevated Split Squat** - `capacity` / `single_leg_strength` / `rear_foot_elevated_split_squat_throwers` - Targets stride-leg strength, hip stability, and asymmetry management with a thrower-relevant split stance.
24. **Lateral Lunge** - `capacity` / `lateral_lower_body_strength` / `lateral_lunge_throwers` - Builds lateral hip strength and adductor tolerance for rotational athletes who load and shift side-to-side.
25. **Single-Leg Romanian Deadlift** - `resilience` / `single_leg_balance_foot_ankle_hip_control` / `single_leg_rdl_throwers` - Trains hamstring-glute strength, hip hinge control, and balance for landing, stride, and fielding transfer.
26. **Hip Thrust** - `capacity` / `posterior_chain_strength` / `hip_thrust_throwers` - Develops hip extension force without loading the shoulder in an overhead position.
27. **Sled Push Acceleration** - `output` / `acceleration_start_speed` / `sled_push_acceleration_throwers` - Builds early acceleration angles and lower-body force projection while keeping running mechanics simple.
28. **Lateral Sled Drag** - `capacity` / `lateral_lower_body_strength` / `lateral_sled_drag_throwers` - Loads lateral hip drive and trunk posture for throwers who need force transfer across the frontal plane.
29. **10-Yard Sprint Start** - `output` / `acceleration_start_speed` / `ten_yard_sprint_start_throwers` - Short acceleration exposure builds nervous-system output and leg drive without excessive running volume.
30. **Lateral Bound to Stick** - `resilience` / `landing_braking_control` / `lateral_bound_to_stick_throwers` - Trains lateral projection, hip capture, knee alignment, and quiet landings before higher-intent lateral power.

# Throwers / Throwing Athletes Exercise Cards 31-40

## Source and authoring basis

- exercise_card_details_for_llm.md: Card v2 authoring workflow, canonical phase keys, movement identity, taxonomy key+weight tags, movement requirements, why layer, coaching execution, dosage, scaling cohorts, pairing logic, safety, regimen, and phase profile.
- Purpose.txt status: requested and searched for, but no accessible File Library result surfaced a file literally titled Purpose.txt during this run. This caveat is preserved in every generated file rather than pretending the file was read.
- Sport-science basis: overhead throwing is treated as a full kinetic-chain task, with selections covering lower body force, hip-pelvis-trunk transfer, scapular control, shoulder/elbow/forearm capacity, rotational power, and fatigue-safe practice design.

## Category focus: Trunk, Pelvis, Anti-Rotation, and Force Transmission
Core and trunk-pelvis drills that teach athletes to transfer force from ground to hand while resisting leaks, over-rotation, extension, and side-bending collapse.

## Exercises in this batch

31. **Pallof Press Iso Hold** - `resilience` / `trunk_pelvis_anti_movement_control` / `pallof_press_iso_hold_throwers` - Teaches the athlete to resist unwanted trunk rotation while breathing and keeping pelvis-rib alignment.
32. **Half-Kneeling Cable Lift** - `movement_intelligence` / `coordinate` / `half_kneeling_cable_lift_throwers` - Trains diagonal force transfer from hip through trunk to hands while the pelvis stays organized.
33. **Half-Kneeling Cable Chop** - `movement_intelligence` / `coordinate` / `half_kneeling_cable_chop_throwers` - Builds controlled trunk rotation and anti-extension in a split stance relevant to throwing posture.
34. **Landmine Anti-Rotation Press** - `resilience` / `trunk_pelvis_anti_movement_control` / `landmine_anti_rotation_press_throwers` - Develops trunk stiffness and scapular upward reach through an angled press that is usually more shoulder-friendly than full overhead pressing.
35. **Cable Anti-Rotation Step-Out** - `resilience` / `trunk_pelvis_anti_movement_control` / `cable_anti_rotation_step_out_throwers` - Adds controlled footwork to anti-rotation so athletes learn to keep trunk position while stepping into and out of tension.
36. **Suitcase Carry** - `capacity` / `carry_trunk_loaded_bracing_strength` / `suitcase_carry_throwers` - Builds lateral trunk stiffness, grip, and gait posture without repetitive throwing stress.
37. **Farmer Carry** - `capacity` / `carry_trunk_loaded_bracing_strength` / `farmer_carry_throwers` - Builds grip, shoulder depression control, trunk stiffness, and total-body work capacity in a simple pattern.
38. **Side Plank Row** - `resilience` / `trunk_pelvis_anti_movement_control` / `side_plank_row_throwers` - Combines lateral trunk control with scapular rowing, useful for throwers who leak through ribs or pelvis while pulling.
39. **Bird Dog Row** - `resilience` / `trunk_pelvis_anti_movement_control` / `bird_dog_row_throwers` - Links contralateral trunk stability, hip control, and scapular pull without speed or impact.
40. **Stir-the-Pot Plank** - `resilience` / `trunk_pelvis_anti_movement_control` / `stir_the_pot_plank_throwers` - Challenges trunk anti-extension and shoulder support under small moving perturbations.

        "default_rpe_max": 6

          "load_guidance": "Use bodyweight, very light medicine ball or band, short range, slow speed, and clear coach demonstration."

          "load_guidance": "Use modest load and simple progressions; prioritize posture, rhythm, and pain-free reps over intensity."

        "adult_advanced": {

        "gender_specific_notes": "Do not assume load from gender. Scale to training age, limb length, joint history, throwing volume, and current readiness."

# Throwers / Throwing Athletes Exercise Cards 41-50

## Source and authoring basis

- exercise_card_details_for_llm.md: Card v2 authoring workflow, canonical phase keys, movement identity, taxonomy key+weight tags, movement requirements, why layer, coaching execution, dosage, scaling cohorts, pairing logic, safety, regimen, and phase profile.
- Purpose.txt status: requested and searched for, but no accessible File Library result surfaced a file literally titled Purpose.txt during this run. This caveat is preserved in every generated file rather than pretending the file was read.
- Sport-science basis: overhead throwing is treated as a full kinetic-chain task, with selections covering lower body force, hip-pelvis-trunk transfer, scapular control, shoulder/elbow/forearm capacity, rotational power, and fatigue-safe practice design.

## Category focus: Shoulder, Scapular, Elbow, and Forearm Capacity
Targeted tissue-capacity work for the cuff, scapular stabilizers, elbow, wrist, and forearm that supports repeated throwing without replacing skill-specific throwing exposure.

## Exercises in this batch

41. **Prone Y-T-W Raise** - `resilience` / `scapular_wrist_hand_support_resilience` / `prone_y_t_w_raise_throwers` - Builds low-load scapular retraction, upward rotation, and posterior shoulder control for throwers.
42. **Face Pull to External Rotation** - `resilience` / `scapular_wrist_hand_support_resilience` / `face_pull_to_external_rotation_throwers` - Combines upper-back pull with external rotation control without heavy pressing stress.
43. **Cable or Band 90/90 External Rotation** - `resilience` / `scapular_wrist_hand_support_resilience` / `cable_band_90_90_external_rotation_throwers` - Builds cuff strength and control in the abducted position used near the arm-cocking phase.
44. **Eccentric Band External Rotation** - `resilience` / `slow_eccentric_isometric_joint_resilience` / `eccentric_band_external_rotation_throwers` - Emphasizes slow external-rotation lowering to support deceleration tolerance after ball release.
45. **Band Shoulder Internal Rotation Decel Control** - `resilience` / `slow_eccentric_isometric_joint_resilience` / `band_internal_rotation_decel_control_throwers` - Trains controlled shoulder rotation through a safe range so the athlete owns the motion instead of snapping through it.
46. **Bottoms-Up Kettlebell Carry** - `resilience` / `scapular_wrist_hand_support_resilience` / `bottoms_up_kettlebell_carry_throwers` - Builds reflexive cuff, scapular, wrist, and grip stability with low reps and high attention.
47. **Landmine Press** - `capacity` / `upper_body_push_strength` / `landmine_press_throwers` - Strengthens pressing and upward reach on an angled path that many throwers tolerate better than vertical pressing.
48. **Chin-Up or Assisted Chin-Up** - `capacity` / `upper_body_pull_strength` / `chin_up_assisted_chin_up_throwers` - Builds lat, upper-back, grip, and shoulder control when the athlete can keep ribs and neck organized.
49. **Wrist Pronation-Supination Hammer Control** - `resilience` / `slow_eccentric_isometric_joint_resilience` / `wrist_pronation_supination_hammer_control_throwers` - Targets forearm pronation-supination control for elbow and wrist tolerance in repeated throwing.
50. **Forearm Flexor/Extensor Eccentric** - `resilience` / `slow_eccentric_isometric_joint_resilience` / `forearm_flexor_extensor_eccentric_throwers` - Builds local forearm tolerance through slow eccentrics, useful as support work for high-volume throwers.
